That\xe2\x80\x99s up from 195.6 in the previous seven days (412 cases in the week to 4 October).</p>\n<div class="g g-2"><div class="g-single a-4"><div class="ipa ipa-adsense mt-2 mb-4">\r\n    <div class="text-center"><script async src="https://pagead2.googlesyndication.com/pagead/js/adsbygoogle.js"></script>\r\n<!-- In-post single -->\r\n<ins class="adsbygoogle"\r\n     style="display:block"\r\n     data-ad-client="ca-pub-4193607936331778"\r\n     data-ad-slot="4973670406"\r\n     data-ad-format="auto"\r\n     data-full-width-responsive="true"></ins>\r\n<script>\r\n     (adsbygoogle = window.adsbygoogle || []).push({});\r\n</script></div>\r\n</div></div></div>\n<p>At the\xc2\xa0<strong>University of York</strong>, there were <strong>324</strong> individuals self isolating due to a positive Covid-19 test on Thursday, up from 288 the day before.</p>\n<p>At\xc2\xa0<strong>York St John University</strong> there were <strong>74 </strong>people self isolating due to a positive test on Wednesday. The rating for York is now Amber. It was Green last week.</p>\n<p><strong>Testing:</strong> As at 5 October, the seven-day positivity rate in York (Pillar 2 only) was 11.57% (447 positives out of 3,864 tests). That\xe2\x80\x99s up from 5.21% last week. The national and regional averages are 7.1% and 10.7% respectively. The number of Pillar 2 tests being carried out in York is increasing.</p>\n<p>The Fulford, Heslington and University MSOA (see table above) is in the top 5% in the Yorkshire and Humber Region for new cases per 100,000 in the seven day period up to 2.10.20.</p>\n<p><strong>Contact tracing:\xc2\xa0</strong>Since 28 May, 1,003 laboratory-confirmed Covid cases in York have been uploaded into the NHS Test and Trace system and 703 of the cases have been engaged. Altogether 2,609 \xe2\x80\x98contacts\xe2\x80\x99 have been identified and 1,699 of these have been traced.</p>\n<p><strong>Deaths:</strong> In the ONS data up to 25 September, <strong>172</strong> deaths were recorded as having occurred for York residents (83 in hospital, 77 in care homes, 9 at home and 3 in a hospice). The numbers have started to fall in the last few days after a very steep rise over the previous two to three weeks with a peak of <strong>653</strong> triages in the 7 day period to 20 September.</p>\n<p><strong>Exceedance: </strong>The PHE \xe2\x80\x98Exceedance\xe2\x80\x99 rating compares the number of new cases over a 14 day period with the previous six weeks and provides a red-amber-green rating to indicate if the trend is worsening. The rating for York is now Green. It was Amber last week.</p>\n<p><strong>Testing:</strong> As at 28 September, the seven-day positivity rate in York (Pillar 2 only) was 5.21% (161 positives out of 3,092 tests). That&#8217;s up from 3.19% last week. The national and regional averages are 4.4 % and 6.0% respectively. The number of Pillar 2 tests being carried out in York is increasing.</p>\n<p><strong>Contact tracing:\xc2\xa0</strong>Since 28 May, 475 laboratory-confirmed Covid cases in York have been uploaded into the NHS Test and Trace system and 377 of the cases have been engaged. Altogether 1,295 \xe2\x80\x98contacts\xe2\x80\x99 have been identified and 842 of these have been traced.</p>\n<div class="g g-1"><div class="g-single a-12"><div class="ipa">\r\n    <div That\xe2\x80\x99s up from <strong>9.0</strong> in the previous seven days (19 cases in the week to 31 August).</p>\n<p>In North Yorkshire, <strong>33</strong> new cases were confirmed today, taking the cumulative total to <strong>2,947</strong> \xe2\x80\x93 an infection rate of 476.8 cases per 100K.</p>\n<p>There are 152 cases in Ryedale (up one), 392 in Selby (up five), 850 in Harrogate (up 14), 350 in Hambleton (up three), 618 in Scarborough (up five), 293 in Richmondshire (up one) and 292 in Craven (up four).</p>\n<div class="g g-2"><div class="g-single a-4"><div class="ipa ipa-adsense mt-2 mb-4">\r\n    <div class="text-center"><script async src="https://pagead2.googlesyndication.com/pagead/js/adsbygoogle.js"></script>\r\n<!-- In-post single -->\r\n<ins class="adsbygoogle"\r\n     style="display:block"\r\n     data-ad-client="ca-pub-4193607936331778"\r\n     data-ad-slot="4973670406"\r\n     data-ad-format="auto"\r\n     data-full-width-responsive="true"></ins>\r\n<script>\r\n     (adsbygoogle = window.adsbygoogle || []).push({});\r\n</script></div>\r\n</div></div></div>\n<p>There were no more coronavirus related deaths reported by York Teaching Hospital NHS Foundation Trust reported today \xe2\x80\x93 the total remains at <strong>214</strong>.
